 Traditional Dance Garba Now Famous People Of Other Religions Around The World Keep Away From Garba: Garba Dance is celebrated in Gujarat during Bajrang Dalnavaratri, and people celebrate this festival fiercely, the special thing is that not only Hindus in this Garba dance Rather people from other religions also participate
 lekin ab is lokapriy garba dance ko lekar bajrang dal ne farmaan jari kiya he ki duusare majahab ke log garba se dur rahen
 In Gujarat, Bajrang Dal has issued a new decree regarding Garba
 bajrang dal ne duusare dharm ke logon ko garba kii jagah se dur rahane ko kaha he
 According to Bajrang Dal, people of other religions make Hindu girls a victim of love jihad
 lagaae kai binargarba se anya dharm ke logon ko dur rahane ke liye bajrang dal ke kaaryakartaaon ne garba sthal, college or uniwarsity ke aasapaas isse sambandhit kai binar lagaae hai
 Garba, the traditional dance of Gujarat is famous all over the world and is celebrated with pomp at many places even outside the state
 gujarat main hi ahmedabad, gandhinagar, rajkot, surat, vadodara, bhavnagar jaise kai bade shaharon main bade str par garba kaa aayojan kiya jaataa he

 'tippaniyan This incident is of a test match played between India and England in February 1980
 mumbai (tab bombai) ke vankhede stadium main khele gaye is golden jubilee test main pehle batting karte hue bhartiya team pehali pari main mahaj 242 ranon par out ho gai thi
 In response, a trio of Indian fast bowlers, Kapil Dev, Karsan Ghavri and Roger Binny had spoiled England's debut as well
 ek samay england ke paanch ballebaaj 58 ran par out ho gaye the
 At this time, all-rounder Ian Botham and wicket-keeper batsman Bob Taylor were partnering to help the England team, while Taylor was playing for 43, then on the bowling of Kapil Dev, the Indian team appealed for a catch behind the wicket and the umpire called him out
 given
 ampire ke faisle ke baavjood bob tailor khud ko out nahin maanate hue krij par khadey rahe
 Viswanath, seeing this situation, went to Taylor and asked him if your bat had an edge, Taylor refused, then Vishi requested the umpire to change the decision
 vishwanath kii is mahaan pahal par bob tailor ko phir se ballebaaji kaa mauka mila
 By the way, it is a different matter that the botham-taylor pair changed the picture of the match by sharing 171 runs for the sixth wicket
 botham ne is match menmen 114 or tailor ne 43 ran banaae
 England's first innings ended with 296 runs and a 54-run lead
 duusari pari main bhartiya team england ke tej gendbaaj ian botham (48 ran dekar saat wicket) ke aage mahaj 149 ran par dher ho gai thi
 In the match, England had a target of 96 runs to win, which they achieved without losing any wicket

 ) a half-century from captain Gautam Gambhir and an all-round performance by Jack Kallis helped the Kolkata Knight Riders continue their unbeaten campaign in the Indian Premier League and beat Chennai Super Kings by five wickets here today

 gambhir ne iske baad manoj tiwari (13) ke saath milakar pari ko aage badhaayaa

 morkal ne haalanki tiwari ko yo mahesh ke haathon kaich kara diya

 isse pehle tas jitkar ballebaaji karne utre chennai kii shuruuaat kharaab rahi or usne paanch over main 32 ran tak hi donon salaami ballebaajon phalf du plasis (03) or mike hasi (18) ke wicket ganvaa die
 Plessis was caught by wicketkeeper Brandon mccullum off paceman Brett Lee in the second over of the innings while Hussey, who was associated with the team, returned to the pavilion to take the run after Australia's West Indies tour ended

 Bravo, however, could not take advantage of this life and was caught by Abdullah at long on in an attempt to pick up the ball from Kallis
 tippaniyan Kolkata bowlers, meanwhile, began to clamp down on the Chennai batsmen and there were no fours or sixes for 46 balls
